                                    </div>

                                        -
                                    </div>

        2003 round 6 #187 overall by Minnesota Wild
    </a>

                                                    <div class="ep-card__body">
                                                                                                        <p class="ep-text mb-2">
                                        Kop&#345;iva is a big goalie who covers a lot of net. Has excellent agility and quick reflexes. Stands on his feet more than your typical butterfly netminder. Has a very strong mental game, but could improve his stickhandling skills.<br>- Ulf Andersson, EP
                                    </p>
